03/10/22, 11:50 - Ravi Bits: #include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;


int Piggybank(vector<int> array){
    int subsum,money = 0;
    int siz=array.size();
    for(int z=0;z<siz;z++){
        int min = *min_element(array.begin(),array.end());
        int mindex = find(array.begin(),array.end(),min)-array.begin();
        subsum = array[mindex];
        cout << "Array[i]:" << subsum << endl;
        if(mindex-1 != -1){
            subsum = subsum*array[mindex-1];
            cout << "Array[i-1]*Array[i]:" << subsum << endl;

        }
        if(mindex+1 != array.size()){
            subsum = subsum*array[mindex+1];
            cout << "Array[i-1]*Array[i]*Array[i+1]:" << subsum << endl;
        }
        array.erase(array.begin()+mindex);
        money = money + subsum;
    }
    cout << endl;
    return(money);
}
int main(){
    int N,n;
    cout << "ENter the number of elements you want in the vector:";
    cin >> N;
    vector<int> banks;
    for(int i = 0;i<N;i++){
        int n;
        cin >> n;
        banks.push_back(n); 
    }
    cout << Piggybank(banks) << endl;
}

03/10/22, 13:19 - Ravi Bits: Q2.PiggyBank
You are given an Array of Piggybanks,<a[6,1,2,3]> if you break ith piggy bank you receive the sum a[i-1]*a[i]*a[i+1],If the i is going out of bounds u just get $1.
03/10/22, 13:20 - Ravi Bits: i.e.  if you break 0th piggy bank you get 1*6*2
03/10/22, 13:20 - Ravi Bits: the broken piggy bank is removed from the array of piggy banks
03/10/22, 13:21 - Ravi Bits: you have to proceed in such a way that you you receive maximum money...

09/07/23, 19:23 - Sandya Bits: Regarding the mock interviews, we (Placement Unit) associated with "Masai School", which conducted mock interviews of two of our own batchmates. This organization basically maps students to people working in SDE-1 and SDE-2 profiles of reputable companies like Microsoft, Amazon, Adobe etc, who take the interviews on a certain platform. Based on the positive response we got from the students and after negotiating the prices with Masai as best as we could, thereâ€™re two pricing models available now:

1.	1 mock interview with feedback costing around 1800/-
2.	2 mock interviews with feedback and considerable time in between the two for improvement scope costing around 2500/-
09/07/23, 19:24 - Sandya Bits: It is understandable that some of you might find the prices excessive but do consider the fact that these interviews will be of top quality and be a great help to your preparation.


If you are opting out of the mock interview because you are confident enough to crack the actual ones yourself, thatâ€™s great!


But if you are backing out of the interviews based on the price, then please remember that the current market conditions are not at all favourable and there's going to be a tough competition for the roles we all aspire especially with the undergraduates, who we all can agree are far more prepared.
